'''Write a function to convert more than one list to nested dictionary.'''
def nested_dict(**kwargs):
    '''
    Convert a dictionary to nested dictionary.
    '''
    new_dict = {}
    for key, value in kwargs.items():
        new_dict[key] = value
    return new_dict


# Test
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3))
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3, d=4))

'''Write a function to convert more than one list to nested dictionary.'''
def nested_dict(**kwargs):
    '''
    Convert a dictionary to nested dictionary.
    '''
    new_dict = {}
    for key, value in kwargs.items():
        new_dict[key] = value
    return new_dict

    Convert a dictionary to nested dictionary.
    '''
    new_dict = {}
    for key, value in kwargs.items():
        new_dict[key] = value
    return new_dict


# Test
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3))
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3, d=4))
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3, d=4, e=5))

'''Write a function to convert more than one list to nested dictionary.'''
def nested_dict(**kwargs):
    '''
    Convert a dictionary to nested dictionary.
    '''
    new_dict = {}
    for key, value in kwargs.items():
        new_dict[key] = value
    return new_dict


# Test
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3))
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3, d=4))
print(nested_dict(a=1, b=2, c=3, d=4, e=5))
